<h3>Tackling Tobacco Program</h3>
<p>A step-by-step program to reduce smoking related harm in vulnerable communities.</p>

<h3>Quitting smoking</h3>
<p>Quitting smoking is an important step in reducing your risk of cancer.</p>
<p><a class="button button-primary" href="http://cancersa.org.au/prevention/smoking/quit-smoking/" target="">Read more</a></p>

<h3>Second-hand smoke</h3>
<p>Learn about the impacts of second-hand smoke and how to reduce your risk.</p>
<p><a class="button button-primary" href="https://www.cancersa.org.au/prevention/smoking/second-hand-smoke/" target="">Read more</a></p>

<h3>Smoke-free environments</h3>
<p>Smoke-free environments help to protect people from second-hand smoke.</p>
<p><a class="button button-primary" href="https://www.cancersa.org.au/prevention/smoking/smoke-free-environments/" target="">Read more</a></p>

<h3>Smoking and COVID-19</h3>
<p>People who smoke are more likely to be impacted by COVID-19.</p>
<p><a class="button button-primary" href="https://www.cancersa.org.au/prevention/smoking/smoking-and-covid-19/" target="">Read more</a></p>

bYWHwf">Cancer Council South Australia acknowledges and pays respect to the Traditional Owners of the lands and waterways on which we live and work. We extend that respect to all Elders, past and present, as well as all other Aboriginal and Torres Strait Islander Peoples. Cancer Council SA recognises that improved cancer outcomes are more likely to be achieved when Aboriginal and Torres Strait Islander Peoples have a say in matters that affect them.<br>
We acknowledge that Aboriginal & Torres Strait Islander Peoples have a unique spiritual connection to Country and we are committed to reconciliation and embedding this in the culture and operations of Cancer Council SA.
